7a1(1): // bshad do cog kyang thos par mi 'gyur/ 'khor de dag kyang tshogs 'dus mi 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das shA kye thub pa'i gdan khri dang / gser gyi me tog khyad par can la bzhugs
7a2(1): pa yang mthong bar 'gyur ro// de bas na khyed rnams 'jig rten der song la/ sangs rgyas de mthong zhing the tshom dag zhun/ khyed rnams kyang bsod nams thob la skye bo// kun la phan pa
7a3(1): dang / bde bar 'gyur ro// de skad ces bka' stsal ma thag du phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing re re nas/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba phrag bcur rang rang gi gnas nas langs te/ 
7a4(1): sa su'i sangs la phyag 'tshal nas/ thabs cig tu dong sa/ byang chub sems dnga' re re yang rol mo rnam pa brgya stong thogs te/ me tog rin po che mchog tu babang po'i char pa ban
7a5(1): bcom ldan 'das shAkya thab pa kAl bder byin te/ bcom ldan 'das la phyag 'tshal nas lan bdun panor ba byas te/ phyogs gcig tu 'dug// denas so so nas tshig ga
7a6(1): dang / ngag gcig dang sgra cig gis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cig gsol zhing zhu bzhi ga mchis na/ skye bo rnams la sman pa dang
7a7(1): 'di nga'i skang du bcom ldan gyis skabs byezhing bshad par ston to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis pas byin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams la bka'i skal pa/ rigs kyi
7a8(1): dga'i chom mngon dbyen rnaMs shig dang / ngas byed rnams la bye brag bye bar bshang ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis/ bcom ldan 'das la 'dzin pas
7b1(1): gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag de bzhin gshegs pas ni/ theg pa cig las mi bshad na/ 'di ni bcom ldan 'das kyis ci'i slad theg pa gsum du bshad ces
7b2(1): gsol ba dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das thogs pa med pa'i ye shes kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams la bka' spel pa/ rigs kyi bu khyed rnams sems can
7b3(1): la phan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir don 'di lta bu 'dri ba legs kyis nyon cig/ rigs kyi bu rnams dper na/ mi gcig la ming gsum yod pa lta bu ste/ chu ngu'i chen byis pa
7b4(1): zhes byalo nyi shu yan chad la sgros bu zhes bya/ lo brgyad cu yan chad 'das pa na rgan po zhes bya'o// nga'i theg pa gsum yang de yang de 'dra ste/ sems rgya chu ngu nyan thos dang / 
7b5(1): theg pa chu ngur bstan na/ sems brgya'abring po rang sangs rgyas tsam la ni theg pa 'bring po bstan/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po theg pa chen po chen po la zhugs pa rnams la ni/ 
7b6(1): theg pa chen po bstan to// rigs kyi bu khyed rnams nyon cig/ mdor mtha' gnyis med pa dang / phyogs gcig tu mthun te/ shes pa'i sgo tha dad kyang / mtha' gcig
7b7(1): du'adra'o// mdor nu theg pa gcig ste/ thabs spyod pa gsum du bgos so// nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa yang / theg pa chen po'i nang du 'du/ theg pa chen po ni/ 
7b8(1): sangs rgyas kyi theg pa'o// de bas na theg pa gsum yong ldeg pa gsum yang theg pa gcig go// zhes chos 'di bstan pa'i che/ byang chu sems dpa' stong phrag bcu mi skye ba'i chos
8a1(1): la 'bod pa thob bo// dge slong brgyad bar+d+ha ni dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu thob bo// lci khri ni chos kyi mig rnam par dag pa thob bo// mi khri rtsa
8a2(1): brgya stong mod la bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do// de nas phyogs bcu nas byin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de
8a3(1): logs su thal mo snar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan bdag cag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mthu dang / byin gyis brlabs kyis
8a4(1): khams 'dir byin cing / bcom ldan 'das kyi zhal mthong ba'i steng du/ theg pa chen rje ma chos kyang thos na/ chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bdag cag gis blangs te/ gzung
8a5(1): su 'dzin par gnas par mdzang dugs pa// de bzhin gshegs pa mya ngan las 'das pa'i slad na/ 'jig rten 'di dang 'jig rten gzhan du ri dang / nags tshal dang / shing drung dang / 
8a6(1): rig pa 'dzin pa'i gnas dang grong khyer dang / zong rdam dang / ljongs dang / dgon pa dang / drar khrod dang / mchod ni dang / btsug lagabang dang / dpe 'dun gyi
8a7(1): / sa don du'is mang po'ad ba dang / rkye du mas so'i kyim du ra ba shing / rgyu mi ma sun sa rnam thas 'angs
8a8(1): nas nas/ ngana' ma ldan pags par bgyu // sngon zhin gags thams dngul ngazhi nam checad ces rab te// gang gis pa sa tshig gcig badzinan/ 
8b1(1): rnams rtag tu dga' ba dang / tshim pa skyes te/ rtag tu sen bkur bgyid cing rang bzhin gyis dge bskyong ngo // gang las thar pa chen po phyogs su rgyas pa'i mdo 'di thos te/ 
8b2(1): dga' ba skyes nas dad pa dang / gus pa'i sems kyis yi ger 'dri ba dang / yi ger 'drir 'jug dam/ glog gam/ kha ton du byas sam/ zung ngam 'chang ngam/ phyag
8b3(1): 'tshal zhing chos kyi rnam grangs 'di nang gi sangs rgyas kyi mtshan gcig gam/ byang chub sems dpa'i ming gcig brjod na/ gang za gde ni tshe 'di nyid la bde bathob ste/ 
8b4(1): sdig pa rnams mi mthong zhing che zad de 'chi 'phos na yang / byang chub sems dpa' bdag cag rnams kyis sngon du lam drang ste/ bdag cag gi 'jig rten gyi khams cig tu skye bar
8b5(1): bgyi'o// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ mdo sde 'di blangs pa dang / gzungs su 'dzin pa'i slad du'o// mdo sde 'di blang ste/ gzungs su 'dzin pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi sku 'dzin pa'o/ 
8b6(1): sangs rgyas kyi sku 'dzin pa ni/ byang chub sems dpa' legs par mngon te/ de bas na de dag ni bdag cag dang bslab cig go// rgyu dang rkyen des ni mdo sde 'di gzugs su 'dzin
8b7(1): pa rnams gnas gcig tu skye zhing mi thal bar smon to// de nas tshangs pa chen po dang / sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lha rnams dang / 'jig rten skyong ba brgyal po chen po bzhi dang / gsang ba
8b8(1): bdag po lag na rdo rje dang / gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po yang dag shes la sogs pa pa dang / klu'i rgyal po dga' bo dang / her dga' bo dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha'
10a1(1): snru kyirnam can dus drug du/ thog ma mgo bcugs nas/ nyin nag bdun par kun shing mangs 'di bzugs / sems mi 'cher
10a2(1): dang / ngan mi g.yeng ba dang / rdeg pa 'i yang ba dang / gags mags dang / bsam pa ma g.yeng ba dang / gzungs su 'dzin pa mi g.yeng ba dang / spyod pa ma
10a3(1): ba dang / bstan cing bslab pa mi g.yeng bar nyin mtshan dus drug du mdo sde 'di'i nang nas 'byung ba/ sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / mdo sde bcu ga

10b1(1): me chen po dang / rlung chen po dang / nyi ma chen po dang / nam mkha' chen po'o// mdo sde 'di ni chen po dang 'dra ste/ gtsang me dang bzang ngan thams cad theg par byed do// 
10b2(1): mdo sde 'di ni chu chen po 'dra ste/ smre stsogs thams cad 'khru bar byed do// mdo sde 'di chen po 'dra ste/ nyon mongs pa dang / sdog pa dang / ldan ljin thams cad tshig par byed
10b3(1): mdo sde 'di rlung chen po dang 'dra ste/ smre srog thams cad 'byed par byed do// mdo sde 'di ni nyi ma chen po dang 'dra ste/ mun nag yod do cog snang bar byed do// mdo sde 'dzin
10b4(1): nam mkha' dang 'dra ste/ babang ngan yod do cog thams cad shong bar byed do// de lta bu'i theg pa chen po'i mdo sde thar pa chen po'i mdo sde thar pa chen po phyogs su rgyas pa 'di
10b5(1): che ba ni dpe zla med do// yang byang chub sems dpa' dang / bar du nyan thos dang / tha mar 'jig tshogs kyi gzugs can yod do// cog mi shong ba med do// de bas khyod
10b6(1): rnams kyis mdo sde 'di gzungs su bzung ste/ 'chongs shig/ kun tu spel bar bgyis shig/ dad cing gus par byos shig dang / khyed la byang chub sems dpa' sems
10b7(1): dpa' chen po rnams sangs rgyas kyi ye shes su chud pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid mngon du thob par bya'o// khyed lha rnams kyang mdo sde 'di blangs ste/ 'chang na rgyun du
11a1(1): nga yang mthong na/ ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor pa dang / dkyil 'khor chen po la zhugs
11a2(1): par bya'o// de nas 'khor mang po'i nang nas/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshan nyid dam zhes bya ba de 'khor 'dus pa'i nang nas stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu ba
11a3(1): nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi nabasal mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag rnams la gsol zhing /

11a5(1): byang chub sems dpa' mtshan nyid dad pa la bka' stsal pa/ shin tu legs so legs so// rigs kyi bu 'dri ba yod na ci 'dod pa bzhin dris shig dang / ngas khyod la bye zag byed
11a6(1): ra bshad do// khyod dris pa de yang sems can dpag tu med pal phan pa dang / bde bar 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub sems dpa' mtshan nyid dad kyis/ bcom ldan 'ad
11a7(1): la 'di rgyud ces gsal to// bdag dran pa ston dun ring po 'das pan/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan nyin chen bcu ga pung dkris bgyi ba de'i mtshan lan cig yos na/ 
11a8(1): skye ba ces pas te/ de la thun mo ring bzhig ni/ rgyal po rtsi'i dbang phyug 'od kyi yul khams na/ dgon pa'i nani ga rji chen po ni ga mchis pa'i cha bsams nas/ 
11b1(1): den ga chen po stong phrag bcu zhig mchis pa gdugs kyis gdungs te/ rgyal ba lta gum du nye ba lA rngam chu'abebs zhes bgyi bas/ de mthong nas/ sems shin tu byams pa dang / 
11b2(1): snying rje skyes te/ tsha ba dang kha zas stsal kyang / dgung 'gal tsam/ gson grang na/ tshe ring por mi thogs par 'tshal bas/ bcom ldan 'das rin chen gtsug phud kyi mtshan lan
11b3(1): gsum brjod nas/ nyade dag thos ma thag tu dus las 'das te/ sum cu rtsa gsum gyi lhar skyes so zhes gda' na/ deng bcom ldan 'das 'khor 'di dag dang / dus pa
11b4(1): ma'i sems can rnams kyi skad du/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi mtshan bstan cing / bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa'i mtshan thos na/ chad ma mchis dpag tum mchis pa'i skye
11b5(1): bo la sman pa dang / bde ba dang / dpag tu ma mchis pa'i bsod nams dang / rtag tu longs spyod phun sum tshogs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid kyang / 
11b6(1): mngon sum du rtogs par 'gyur ba'i slad du gsol lo// sdom pa'i rtsa ba nyams pa dang / nyon mongs pas 'khrul pa'i sems can rnams yongs su grol bar 'gyur ba'i
11b7(1): slad du bshad du smon to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po mtshan nyid la 'dod pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu gal te
11b8(1): ngas phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi mtshan rgya cher bshad na/ bskal pa brgya khri'i bar du shad pas kyang mi rdzogs te/ 'di ltar chu thams cad kyi rigs pa ni bgrang shing shes pa

12a3(1): gsum gyi sangs rgyas rnams kyis mtshan mdo tsam zhig bstan gyis/ gang gi rnam par lan cig na/ gang zag de tshe 'phos ma thag tu lha'i gnas su skye bar 'gyur/ thos nas kyang

13a1(1): phyir zhe na/ 'jigs tshogs can kun la sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid yod pa'i phyir ro// kye 'khor mang po rnams sor mo bcu'i thal mo sbyor la yang

13a3(1): lnga po yang // rnam grol mtshan nyid bskyed par bya// dge rtsa med pa'i gang zag la// ngas ni grol zhing bshad kyis kyang // des kyang chud par mi nus te// sa bon tshig rnams

14a7(1): phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas gsar mdzod la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas sa'i gdung la brag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas zla ba'i gzugs 'arjod la phyag 'tshal la/ 
14a8(1): sangs rgyas ni ma'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas pad+ma rnam grol la phyag 'tshal mo// sangs rgyas 'od gzer rnam can la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas
14b1(1): tho na mtsho mngon par shes la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas chu 'od la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas dbyangs chen la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas jim sgyum dang thal la bya
14b2(1): 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas yid skyo spangs la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas rin po che 'bar byal phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas gtsug dam pa la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs
14b3(1): rgyas dpa' 'bar 'dzugs pa la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas shes rab yon tan 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas nyi zla 'od sgribs la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rdza
14b4(1): nyi zla bai DUr+ya'i 'od la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas bla med bai DUr+ya'i 'od la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas rab mchog gtso la phyag 'tshal lo// sangs rgyas byang chub me tog

203b2(1): chos tshol ba la brtson pas ngan du brjod pa dang / ngan du smra ba'i tshig gi lam brjod pa dang / chos tshol ba la brtson pas/ rlung dang / nyim dang / grang ba dang / tshad
203b3(1): bkres pa dang / skom pa bzod pa dang / chos tshol ba la brtson pas/ mkhan po dang / slob dpon dang / mthun par 'jug pa'i bzod pa dang / chos tshol ba la brtson pas
203b4(1): stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'i chos la bzod pa dang / bzod pa bzhi po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par 'gyuraro// 
203b5(1): brtson 'grus bzhi po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ nyan pa'i brtson 'grus dang / 'dzin
203b6(1): ba'i brtson 'grus dang / bstan pa'i brtson 'grus dang / nan tan gyi brtson 'grus dang / brtson 'grus bzhi po de dag ni byang sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par
203b7(1): 'gyur ro// bsam gtan gyi yan lag bzhi po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur te/ gzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ dben pa dang / 
203b8(1): rtse gcig pa dang / bsam gtan dang / mngon par shes pa chos 'das/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la rten pa ste/ bsam gtan gyi yan 'ag ni po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems
204a1(1): dpa' rnams kyi shes kyis tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur ro// shes rab kyi snang ba bzhi po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshogs
204a2(1): rdzogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ba ste/ chad pa la mi gnas pa dang / rtag pa la mi 'jug pa dang / rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba dang mi 'gal ba dang / bdag
204a3(1): med la bzod pa ste/ shes rab kyi snang ba bzhi po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur ro// thabs bzhi po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnam
204a4(1): kyi ye shes kyi tshogs rdzogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi rjes su 'jug pa dang / sems can gyi rjes su 'jug pa dang / chos kyi rjes su 'jug
204a5(1): pa dang / ye shes kyis rjes su 'jug pa sted / thabs bzhi po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs sogs par 'gyur ro// lam bzhi po 'di dag
204a6(1): ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs sogs par 'gyur te/ bani gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i lam dang / sa'i lam dang / byang chub kyi chos
204a7(1): kyi lam dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyis lam ste/ lam bzhi po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyis tshogs sogs par 'gyur ro// mi ngoms pa
204a8(1): bzhi po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi tshogs sogs par 'gyur te/ bzhi gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ thos pa'i mi ngoms pa dang / bstan pas mi mas pa
